take your insurance plan. After you\'ve searched for doctors by specialty, click the &quot;Insurance&quot; option in the search filter and then select your specific insurance provider. </div></div><div data-v-270d6519><div class="question" data-v-270d6519><b data-v-270d6519> How can I schedule a virtual visit (video visit) with a Pediatrician in Los Angeles? </b> <br data-v-270d6519></div><div class="answer" data-v-270d6519> If you\'re looking to schedule a video appointment instead of seeing a doctor in person, doctors who meet with patients online will have a &quot;Virtual Visit&quot; button at the top of their WebMD Care profile page. </div></div><div data-v-270d6519><div class="question" data-v-270d6519><b data-v-270d6519> How can I find top-rated Pediatricians near me in Los Angeles? </b> <br data-v-270d6519></div><div class="answer" data-v-270d6519> Finding top-rated Pediatricians near you is simple on WebMD Care.
